56→\t\t\tCreatedAt: created,\n    57→\t\t\tUpdatedAt: created,\n    58→\t\t},\n    59→\t\tflags:        map[string]*flipt.Flag{},\n    60→\t\tsegments:     map[string]*flipt.Segment{},\n    61→\t\trules:        map[string]*flipt.Rule{},\n    62→\t\trollouts:     map[string]*flipt.Rollout{},\n    63→\t\tevalRules:    map[string][]*storage.EvaluationRule{},\n    64→\t\tevalRollouts: 72→func WithValidatorOption(opts ...validation.FeaturesValidatorOption) containers.Option[SnapshotOption] {\n    73→\treturn func(so *SnapshotOption) {\n    74→\t\tso.validatorOption = opts\n    75→\t}\n    76→}\n    77→\n    78→// SnapshotFromFS is a convenience function for building a snapshot\n    79→// directly from an implementation of fs.FS using the list state files\n    80→// function to source the relevant Flipt configuration files.\n    81→func SnapshotFromFS(logger *zap.Logger, src fs.FS, opts ...containers.Option[SnapshotOption]) (*Snapshot, error) {\n    82→\tpaths, err := listStateFiles(logger, src)\n    83→\tif err != nil {\n    84→\t\treturn nil, err\n    85→\t}\n    86→\n    87→\treturn SnapshotFromPaths(logger, src, paths, opts...)\n    88→}\n    89→\n    90→// SnapshotFromPaths constructs a StoreSnapshot from the provided\n    91→// slice of paths resolved against the provided fs.FS.\n    92→func SnapshotFromPaths(logger *zap.Logger, ffs fs.FS, paths []string, opts ...containers.Option[SnapshotOption]) (*Snapshot, error) {\n    93→\tlogger.Debug(\"opening state files\", zap.Strings(\"paths\", paths))\n    94→\n    95→\tvar files []fs.File\n    96→\tfor _, file := range paths {\n    97→\t\tfi, err := ffs.Open(file)\n    98→\t\tif err != nil {\n    99→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   100→\t\t}\n   101→\n   102→\t\tfiles = append(files, fi)\n   103→\t}\n   104→\n   105→\treturn SnapshotFromFiles(logger, files, opts...)\n   106→}\n   107→\n   108→// SnapshotFromFiles constructs a StoreSnapshot from the provided slice\n   109→// of fs.File implementations.\n   110→func SnapshotFromFiles(logger *zap.Logger, files []fs.File, opts ...containers.Option[SnapshotOption]) (*Snapshot, error) {\n   111→\tnow := flipt.Now()\n   112→\ts := Snapshot{\n   113→\t\tns: map[string]*namespace{\n   114→\t\t\tdefaultNs: newNamespace(\"default\", \"Default\", now),\n   115→\t\t},\n   116→\t\tevalDists: map[string][]*storage.EvaluationDistribution{},\n   117→\t\tnow:       now,\n   118→\t}\n   119→\n   120→\tvar so SnapshotOption\n   121→\tcontainers.ApplyAll(&so, opts...)\n   122→\n   123→\tfor _, fi := range files {\n   124→\t\tdefer fi.Close()\n   125→\t\tinfo, err := fi.Stat()\n   126→\t\tif err != nil {\n   127→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   128→\t\t}\n   129→\n   130→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"opening state file\", zap.String(\"path\", info.Name()))\n   131→\n   132→\t\tdocs, err := documentsFromFile(fi, so)\n   133→\t\tif err != nil {\n   134→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   135→\t\t}\n   136→\n   137→\t\tfor _, doc := range docs {\n   138→\t\t\tif err := s.addDoc(doc); err != nil {\n   139→\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   140→\t\t\t}\n   141→\t\t}\n   142→\t}\n   143→\n   144→\treturn &s, nil\n   145→}\n   146→\n   147→// WalkDocuments walks all the Flipt feature documents found in the target fs.FS\n   148→// based on either the default index file or an index file located in the root\n   149→func WalkDocuments(logger *zap.Logger, src fs.FS, fn func(*ext.Document) error) error {\n   150→\tpaths, err := listStateFiles(logger, src)\n   151→\tif err != nil {\n   152→\t\treturn err\n   153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\tfor _, file := range paths {\n   156→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"opening state file\", zap.String(\"path\", file))\n   157→\n   158→\t\tfi, err := src.Open(file)\n   159→\t\tif err != nil {\n   160→\t\t\treturn err\n   161→\t\t}\n   162→\t\tdefer fi.Close()\n   163→\n   164→\t\tdocs, err := documentsFromFile(fi, SnapshotOption{})\n   165→\t\tif err != nil {\n   166→\t\t\treturn err\n   167→\t\t}\n   168→\n   169→\t\tfor _, doc := range docs {\n   170→\t\t\tif err := fn(doc); err != nil {\n   171→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   172→\t\t\t}\n   173→\t\t}\n   174→\t}\n   175→\n   176→\treturn nil\n   177→}\n   178→\n   179→// documentsFromFile parses and validates a document from a single fs.File instance\n   180→func documentsFromFile(fi fs.File, opts SnapshotOption) ([]*ext.Document, error) {\n   181→\tvalidator, err := validation.NewFeaturesValidator(opts.validatorOption...)\n   182→\tif err != nil {\n   183→\t\treturn nil, err\n   184→\t}\n   185→\n   186→\tstat, err := fi.Stat()\n   187→\tif err != nil {\n   188→\t\treturn nil, err\n   189→\t}\n   190→\n   191→\tbuf := &bytes.Buffer{}\n   192→\treader := io.TeeReader(fi, buf)\n   193→\n   194→\tvar docs []*ext.Document\n   195→\textn := filepath.Ext(stat.Name())\n   196→\n   197→\tvar decode func(any) error\n   198→\tswitch extn {\n   199→\tcase \".yaml\", \".yml\":\n   200→\t\t// Support YAML stream by looping until we reach an EOF.\n   201→\t\tdecode = yaml.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n   202→\tcase \"\", \".json\":\n   203→\t\tdecode = json.NewDecoder(buf).Decode\n   204→\tdefault:\n   205→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected extension: %q\", extn)\n   206→\t}\n   207→\n   208→\t// validate after we have checked supported\n   209→\t// extensions but before we attempt to decode the\n   210→\t// buffers contents to ensure we fill the buffer\n   211→\t// via the TeeReader\n   212→\tif err := validator.Validate(stat.Name(), reader); err != nil {\n   213→\t\treturn nil, err\n   214→\t}\n   215→\n   216→\tfor {\n   217→\t\tdoc := &ext.Document{}\n   218→\t\tif err := decode(doc); err != nil {\n   219→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, io.EOF) {\n   220→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   221→\t\t\t}\n   222→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   223→\t\t}\n   224→\n   225→\t\t// set namespace to default if empty in document\n   226→\t\tif doc.Namespace == \"\" {\n   227→\t\t\tdoc.Namespace = \"default\"\n   228→\t\t}\n   229→\t\tdocs = append(docs, doc)\n   230→\t}\n   231→\n   232→\treturn docs, nil\n   233→}\n   234→\n   235→// listStateFiles lists all the file paths in a provided fs.FS containing Flipt feature state\n   236→func listStateFiles(logger *zap.Logger, src fs.FS) ([]string, error) {\n   237→\tidx, err := OpenFliptIndex(logger, src)\n   238→\tif err != nil {\n   239→\t\treturn nil, err\n   240→\t}\n   241→\n   242→\tvar paths []string\n   243→\tif err := fs.WalkDir(src, \".\", func(path string, d fs.DirEntry, err error) error {\n   244→\t\tif err != nil {\n   245→\t\t\treturn err\n   246→\t\t}\n   247→\n   248→\t\tif d.IsDir() {\n   249→\t\t\treturn nil\n   250→\t\t}\n   251→\n   252→\t\tif idx.Match(path) {\n   253→\t\t\tpaths = append(paths, path)\n   254→\t\t}\n   255→\n   256→\t\treturn nil\n   257→\t}); err != nil {\n   258→\t\treturn nil, err\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\treturn paths, nil\n   262→}\n   263→\n   264→func (ss *Snapshot) addDoc(doc *ext.Document) error {\n   265→\tns := ss.ns[doc.Namespace]\n   266→\tif ns == nil {\n   267→\t\tns = newNamespace(doc.Namespace, doc.Namespace, ss.now)\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\tevalDists := map[string][]*storage.EvaluationDistribution{}\n   271→\tif len(ss.evalDists) > 0 {\n   272→\t\tevalDists = ss.evalDists\n   273→\t}\n   274→\n   275→\tfor _, s 284→\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   285→\t\t}\n   286→\n   287→\t\tfor _, constraint := range s.Constraints {\n   288→\t\t\tconstraintType := flipt.ComparisonType_value[constraint.Type]\n   289→\t\t\tsegment.Constraints = append(segment.Constraints, &flipt.Constraint{\n   290→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   291→\t\t\t\tSegmentKey:   segment.Key,\n   292→\t\t\t\tId: flipt.ComparisonType(constraintType),\n   296→\t\t\t\tValue:        constraint.Value,\n   297→\t\t\t\tDescription:  constraint.Description,\n   298→\t\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   299→\t\t\t\tUpdatedAt:    ss.now,\n   300→\t\t\t})\n   301→\t\t}\n   302→\n   303→\t\tns.segments[segment.Key] = segment\n   304→\t}\n   305→\n   306→\tfor _, f := range doc.Flags {\n   307→\t\tflagType := flipt.FlagType_value[f.Type]\n   308→\t\tflag := &flipt.Flag{\n   309→\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n   310→\t\t\tKey:          f.Key,\n   311→\t\t\tName:         f.Name,\n   312→\t\t\tDescription:  f.Description,\n   313→\t\t\tEnabled:      f.Enabled,\n   314→\t\t\tType:         flipt.FlagType(flagType),\n   315→\t\t\tCreatedAt:    ss.now,\n   316→\t\t\tUpdatedAt: 323→\t\t\t}\n   324→\n   325→\t\t\tflag.Variants = append(flag.Variants, &flipt.Variant{\n   326→\t\t\t\tId:           uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String(),\n   327→\t\t\t\tNamespaceKey: doc.Namespace,\n         rank,\n   356→\t\t\t}\n   357→\n   358→\t\t\tswitch s := r.Segment.IsSegment.(type) {\n   359→\t\t\tcase ext.SegmentKey:\n   360→\t\t\t\trule.SegmentKey = string(s)\n   361→\t\t\tcase 416→\t\t\t\tid := uuid.Must(uuid.NewV4()).String()\n   417→\t\t\t\trule.Distributions = append(rule.Distributions, &flipt.Distribution{\n   418→\t\t\t\t\tId:        id,\n   419→\t\t\t\t\tRollout: 435→\t\t\tns.rules[rule.Id] = rule\n   436→\t\t}\n   437→\n   438→\t\tns.evalRules[f.Key] = evalRules\n   439→\n   440→\t\tevalRollouts := make([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, 0, len(f.Rollouts))\n 792→func find[T any](match func(T) bool, ts ...T) (t T, _ bool) {\n   793→\tfor _, t := range ts {\n   794→\t\tif match(t) {\n   795→\t\t\treturn t, true\n   796→\t\t}\n   797→\t}\n   798→\n   799→\treturn t, false\n   800→}\n   801→\n   802→func paginate[T any](params storage.QueryParams, less func(i, j int) bool, items ...T) (storage.ResultSet[T], error) {\n   803→\tif len(items) == 0 {\n   804→\t\treturn storage.ResultSet[T]{}, nil\n   805→\t}\n   806→\n   807→\tset := storage.ResultSet[T]{\n   808→\t\tResults: items,\n   809→\t}\n   810→\n   811→\t// sort by created_at and specified order\n   812→\tsort.Slice(set.Results, func(i, j int) bool {\n   813→\t\tif params.Order != storage.OrderAsc {\n   814→\t\t\ti, j = j, i\n   815→\t\t}\n   816→\n   817→\t\treturn less(i, j)\n   818→\t})\n   819→\n   820→\t// parse page token as an offset integer\n   821→\tvar offset int\n   822→\tv, err := strconv.ParseInt(params.PageToken, 10, 64)\n   823→\tif params.PageToken != \"\" && err != nil {\n   824→\t\treturn storage.ResultSet[T]{}, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"pageToken is not valid: %q\", params.PageToken)\n   825→\t}\n   826→\n   827→\toffset = int(v)\n   828→\n   829→\tif offset >= len(set.Results) {\n   830→\t\treturn storage.ResultSet[T]{}, errs.ErrInvalidf(\"invalid offset: %d\", offset)\n   831→\t}\n   832→\n   833→\t// 0 means no limit on page size (all items from offset)\n   834→\tif params.Limit == 0 {\n   835→\t\tset.Results = set.Results[offset:]\n   836→\t\treturn set, nil\n   837→\t}\n   838→\n   839→\t// ensure end of page does not exceed entire set\n   840→\tend := offset + int(params.Limit)\n   841→\tif end > len(set.Results) {\n   842→\t\tend = len(set.Results)\n   843→\t} else if end < len(set.Results) {\n   844→\t\t// set next page token given there are more entries\n   845→\t\tset.NextPageToken = fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", end)\n   846→\t}\n   847→\n   848→\t// reduce results set to requested page\n   849→\tset.Results = set.Results[offset:end]\n   850→\n   851→\treturn set, nil\n   852→}\n   853→\n   854→func (ss *Snapshot) getNamespace(key string) (namespace, error) {\n   855→\tns, ok := ss.ns[key]\n   856→\tif !ok {\n   857→\t\treturn int(params.Limit)\n\tif end > len(set.Results) {\n\t\tend = len(set.Results)\n\t} else if end < len(set.Results) {\n\t\t// set next page token given there are more entries\n\t\tset.NextPageToken = == 0 {\n\t\treturn storage.ResultSet[T]{}, nil\n\t}\n\n\tset := storage.ResultSet[T]{\n\t\tResults: items,\n\t}\n\n\t// sort by created_at and specified order\n\tsort.Slice(set.Results, func(i, j int) int(params.Limit)\n\tif end > len(set.Results) {\n\t\tend = len(set.Results)\n\t} else if end < len(set.Results) {\n\t\t// set next page token given there are more entries\n\t\tset.NextPageToken =
